```typescript
  returnPct,                                 // ูุณุจุฉ ุงูุนุงุฆุฏ
  currency: 'EGP',                           // ุงูุนููุฉ ุงูุฑุฆูุณูุฉ
  originalCurrency,                          // ุงูุนููุฉ ุงูุฃุตููุฉ
}
```

### ๐จ **2. ุชุญุฏูุซ ุนุฑุถ ุจุทุงูุงุช ุงูุงุณุชุซูุงุฑุงุช ุงููุฑุฏูุฉ**

**ุงูููู ุงููุนุฏู**: `src/app/investments/page.tsx`

#### ๐ฐ **ุนุฑุถ ุงููููุฉ ุงูุญุงููุฉ**:

**ูุซุงู ุงูุนุฑุถ**:

### ๐ง **3. ุชุญุฏูุซ ุฏูุงู ุงูุญุณุงุจ ูู Context**

**ุงูููู ุงููุนุฏู**: `src/contexts/investments-context.tsx`

#### ๐ **ุฏุงูุฉ calculateInvestmentValue ุงููุญุฏุซุฉ**:

```typescript
const calculateInvestmentValue = (investment: Investment): number => {
  // ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุณุนุฑ ุงูุตุฑู ูู localStorage
  const exchangeRate = localStorage.getItem('currentExchangeRate') || 1

  let valueInOriginalCurrency = 0
  let needsConversion = false

  // ุญุณุงุจ ุงููููุฉ ุจุงูุนููุฉ ุงูุฃุตููุฉ
  switch (investment.type) {
    case 'precious_metals':
      valueInOriginalCurrency = investment.quantity * investment.currentPrice
      needsConversion = investment.currency === 'USD'
      break
    case 'cryptocurrency':
      valueInOriginalCurrency = investment.quantity * investment.currentPrice
      needsConversion = true // ุฏุงุฆูุงู USD
      break
    case 'certificate':
      valueInOriginalCurrency = investment.amount
      needsConversion = false // ุฏุงุฆูุงู EGP
      break
    case 'stock':
      valueInOriginalCurrency = investment.shares * investment.currentPrice
      needsConversion = true // ุฏุงุฆูุงู USD
      break
  }

  // ุชุญููู ุฅูู ุงูุฌููู ุฅุฐุง ูุฒู ุงูุฃูุฑ
  return needsConversion ? valueInOriginalCurrency * exchangeRate : valueInOriginalCurrency
}
```

#### ๐ **ุฏุงูุฉ calculateInvestmentCost ุงููุญุฏุซุฉ**:

```typescript
const calculateInvestmentCost = (investment: Investment): number => {
  // ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุณุนุฑ ุงูุตุฑู ูู localStorage
  const exchangeRate = localStorage.getItem('currentExchangeRate') || 1

  let costInOriginalCurrency = 0
  let needsConversion = false

  // ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุชูููุฉ ุจุงูุนููุฉ ุงูุฃุตููุฉ (ุดุงููุฉ ุงูุฑุณูู)
  switch (investment.type) {
    case 'precious_metals':
      costInOriginalCurrency = (investment.quantity * investment.purchasePrice) + (investment.purchaseFee || 0)
      needsConversion = investment.currency === 'USD'
      break
    case 'cryptocurrency':
      costInOriginalCurrency = (investment.quantity * investment.purchasePrice) + (investment.cryptoPurchaseFee || 0)
      needsConversion = true // ุฏุงุฆูุงู USD
      break
    case 'certificate':
      costInOriginalCurrency = investment.amount
      needsConversion = false // ุฏุงุฆูุงู EGP
      break
    case 'stock':
      costInOriginalCurrency = (investment.shares * investment.purchasePrice) + (investment.commission || 0)
      needsConversion = true // ุฏุงุฆูุงู USD
      break
  }

  // ุชุญููู ุฅูู ุงูุฌููู ุฅุฐุง ูุฒู ุงูุฃูุฑ
  return needsConversion ? costInOriginalCurrency * exchangeRate : costInOriginalCurrency
}
```

### 1๏ธโฃ3๏ธโฃ **ุฅุตูุงุญ ูุดููุฉ ุงููุฏููููุฉ ุงููุจุฏุฆูุฉ ููุนููุงุก** ๐ง

**ุงููุตู**: ุฅุตูุงุญ ูุดููุฉ ุนุฏู ุธููุฑ ุงููุฏููููุฉ ุงููุจุฏุฆูุฉ ุนูุฏ ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุนููู ุฌุฏูุฏ

**ุงููุดููุฉ**:

**ุงูุณุจุจ**:

**ุงูุญู**:

#### 1๏ธโฃ ุชุนุฏูู `customers-context.tsx`:

**ูุจู**:
```typescript

    ...customerData,
    totalPurchases: 0,
    totalPayments: 0,

    openingBalance: 0, // ุฏุงุฆูุงู ุตูุฑ
  }
```

**ุจุนุฏ**:

```typescript
    ...customerData,
    totalPurchases: 0,
    totalPayments: 0,

  }
}, [])
```

### 1๏ธโฃ5๏ธโฃ **ุฅุตูุงุญ ูุดููุฉ ุฏูุนุงุช ุงูุนููุงุก ูุง ุชูุฎุตู ูู ุงููุฏููููุฉ** ๐ด

**ุงูุณููู ูุจู ุงูุฅุตูุงุญ**:

```
- ุงููุฏููููุฉ ุจุนุฏ ุงูุฏูุนุฉ: 10,000 ุฌููู โ (ูู ุชุชุบูุฑ!)
```

**ุงูุณุจุจ ุงูุฌุฐุฑู**:
ุงููุดููุฉ ูุงูุช ูู ุชูููุช ุชุญุฏูุซ ุงูุฅุญุตุงุฆูุงุช:
1. ูุงูุช ุฏุงูุฉ `addPayment` ุชุณุชุฏุนู `updateCustomerStats` ุจุนุฏ `setPayments`
2. ููู `setPayments` ูู asynchronousุ ูุฐุง ุนูุฏ ุงุณุชุฏุนุงุก `updateCustomerStats`ุ ูู ุชูู ุงูุฏูุนุฉ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ ููุฌูุฏุฉ ุจุนุฏ ูู state
3. ูุชูุฌุฉ ูุฐููุ ูุงู ุงูุญุณุงุจ ูุชู ุจุฏูู ุงูุฏูุนุฉ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ

**ุงูุญู**:

ุชู ุชุนุฏูู ุฏุงูุฉ `addPayment` ูุชุญุฏูุซ ุฅุญุตุงุฆูุงุช ุงูุนููู **ูุจุงุดุฑุฉ** ุจุฏูุงู ูู ุงูุงุนุชูุงุฏ ุนูู `updateCustomerStats`:

**ูุจู**:
```typescript
const addPayment = useCallback((paymentData) => {
  const newPayment = { ...paymentData, id: '...', createdAt: '...' }

  setPayments(prev => [...prev, newPayment])

  // โ ุงููุดููุฉ: updateCustomerStats ููุณุชุฏุนู ูุจู ุฃู ุชูุญุฏุซ payments
```

**ุจุนุฏ**:
```typescript
const addPayment = useCallback((paymentData) => {
  const newPayment = { ...paymentData, id: '...', createdAt: '...' }

  setPayments(prev => [...prev, newPayment])

  // โ ุงูุญู: ุชุญุฏูุซ ุฅุญุตุงุฆูุงุช ุงูุนููู ูุจุงุดุฑุฉ
  setCustomers(prev => prev.map(customer => {
    if (customer.id === paymentData.customerId) {
      const totalPayments = customer.totalPayments + paymentData.amount

      // ุญุณุงุจ ุงููุฏููููุฉ ุงูุญุงููุฉ
      const customerReturns = returns.filter(ret => ret.customerId === paymentData.customerId)
      const totalReturns = customerReturns.reduce((sum, ret) => sum + ret.amount, 0)
      const currentDebt = customer.openingBalance + customer.totalPurchases - totalPayments - totalReturns

      return {
        ...customer,
        totalPayments,
        currentDebt,
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      }
    }
    return customer
  }))
}, [returns])
```

**ุงูููู ุงููุนุฏู**:
- `src/contexts/customers-context.tsx` - ุฏุงูุฉ `addPayment`

**ุงูุณููู ุจุนุฏ ุงูุฅุตูุงุญ**:
```
- ูุฏููููุฉ ุงูุนููู ุงูุญุงููุฉ: 10,000 ุฌููู
- ุชุณุฌูู ุฏูุนุฉ: 3,000 ุฌููู
- ุงููุฏููููุฉ ุจุนุฏ ุงูุฏูุนุฉ: 7,000 ุฌููู โ (ุชู ุงูุฎุตู ุจูุฌุงุญ!)
```

**ูุนุงุฏูุฉ ุงูุญุณุงุจ**:
```
currentDebt = openingBalance + totalPurchases - totalPayments - totalReturns
currentDebt = 5,000 + 10,000 - 3,000 - 0 = 12,000 ุฌููู
```

**ุงูููุฒุงุช**:
- โ **ุฎุตู ููุฑู**: ุงูุฏูุนุฉ ุชูุฎุตู ูู ุงููุฏููููุฉ ููุฑุงู
- โ **ุญุณุงุจ ุฏููู**: ุงููุนุงุฏูุฉ ุงูุตุญูุญุฉ ุชูุทุจู ุจุดูู ุตุญูุญ
- โ **ุชุญุฏูุซ ุดุงูู**: ูุชู ุชุญุฏูุซ `totalPayments` ู `currentDebt` ูุนุงู
- โ **ูุฑุงุนุงุฉ ุงููุฑุชุฌุนุงุช**: ุงูุญุณุงุจ ูุฃุฎุฐ ูู ุงูุงุนุชุจุงุฑ ุงููุฑุชุฌุนุงุช ุฃูุถุงู

**ุงููุชูุฌุฉ**:
- **ุงููููุงุช ุงููุนุฏูุฉ**: 1
- **ุงูุฏูุงู ุงููุนุฏูุฉ**: 1 (`addPayment`)
- **ุงูุญุงูุฉ**: โ **ุชู ุงูุฅุตูุงุญ ุจุงููุงูู**

### 1๏ธโฃ6๏ธโฃ **ุชุญุณูู ุฅุฎูุงุก ุฃุณูู ุงูุฒูุงุฏุฉ/ุงูุชูููู ูู ุญููู ุงูุฃุฑูุงู** ๐จ
